<resp>None</resp><Text>I was recommended to this place from a friend for eyeglass repair. I put in a call to see if they could fix a pair of my sunglasses for me.

Phone rings: "hotshots"

I said: Hi there, I have a question for you?

No response.

I asked if he could hear me? No response.

Hello, can you hear me? No response.

I assumed we had been disconnected. I hung up and tried again. No answer.

I tried 5 minutes later. "Hotshots"...

Hi, can you hear me ok?

Finally he speaks. "I can hear you", I said "ok because you didn't respond". He became combative and rambled on for 5 minutes telling me "you called and said you had a question, I waited for your question, you didn't ask a question, you hung up on me, you called me, you got voice-mail and didn't leave a message, you called, I answered, you asked if you could hear me, I'm still waiting for your question"...

It was the most baffling exchange I've ever had with a business. Typically when someone says hello and asks "I have a question" you respond with "how can I help you" or "sure go ahead" or something... not complete silence. I didn't know if he was on the line or not and after asking if he could hear me twice, with not a sound out of him. One is only left to assume that the call was disconnected

I was so confused and annoyed by his blatant rudeness that I told him he sounded like a lunatic and have a nice day.

5 minutes later HE CALLED ME with a rambling voicemail "I could tell the second you first spoke that you were an incredibly rude person, and I was right so from one lunatic to the next you have a nice day"

Again, baffled is the only word used to explain how this person does business. When you start off being rude to your guests and then try to turn it around that they are rude. And then call them and leave them harassing voicemails...

If you decide to use this business I would try to keep communication to a minimum because it's clearly something this owner struggles with.< /Text></record>

<user_name>C Loo<//user_name><user>112132534981451547670<//user><Review>My first time here. Was referred here by Costco San Marcos. They gave me a heads up that the guy was not very personable but was good at what he does- repairing glasses. Very interesting as I don't think a lot of people do this type of work.

I had two complicated repairs and maybe one easier one; the easy one was the nose pad broke off the glasses when Costco adjusted them for me. The other two issues were an arm that broke off when the glasses went through a washing machine :(. The third was stripped screws in the arms of a heavy pair of glasses/ loupes. He was able to fix all of them quickly, efficiently and masterly (as someone else noted).

He is really quite busy- constant flow of customers while I was there but is good and fast and stands behind his work as others here on yelp have noted.

There is a front reception area (he is the only one there) where you wait for your glasses repair. He also has a sign with all the fees so you don't have to ask him anything related to fees.  there is a back room area where he does all his work and repairs. The back room says that he can see you and knows you're there (see photo).

You just have to get over that he is not that Personal. He just might have a slight highly functioning autism. He asked me if I had something to tell/ ask him a couple of times cause I guess he can see me through his camera in the back inspecting the glasses. When I told him I did, he said "I knew it". It was a little abrupt but i guess he's pretty smart.  And, as someone else said, I don't need that. I want good quality work that is guaranteed at very reasonable fees!< /Review>< rating>

< Text>
No nonsense repairs...Inexpensive is an understatement.
Fast and very inexpensive. This gentleman has repaired about a dozen pair of glasses
for me, friends and family without any stress and always at very low cost.

You go into the small waiting room at street level and wait for the repair man, Doctor of Frames, the miracle worker to come out of the shop in the back. He hands the repairs to those that are waiting and collects his fees. He takes the next batch of repairs from those waiting. Very little explanation is usually needed, he tells you what the bill will be before hand. He goes in the back with your glasses as well as everyone else's. Fifteen or twenty minutes later he returns. Again, distributes the repairs, collects the money and collects the next round of  repairs. Minimum of chit chat, you bring your repairs, they get repaired you pay and leave,
The impossible repairs are repaired.

There is non better....The service is fast and efficient. Take a lesson in hard work,
the grace of no wasted energy and speed. He is the Bruce Lee of eyeglass repair.<//Text>

Where has this place been all my life?
I stumbled upon this shop on my way to lunch and decided to pop in as I had recently replaced a broken pair of frames with a new pair of the same exact frame but my lenses didn't fit perfectly for some reason and would pop out sometimes. I walked in an saw about 5 people waiting and no owner in sight.  One of the people waiting informed me that the owner was in the back and would be right out.  When he came out he was super friendly and I explained my situation.  He took my glasses, came back within 5 minutes and they were perfect... and the best part, my adjustment was at no charge.

I can't believe people review this guy as being rude! I mean I can understand him being a little abrupt when he has 5 people waiting but I wouldn't call him rude!

Bottom line is, if you have a broken pair of glasses and 20 minutes then this is a great place to go.<//Text>

<text>First a little background info.  I purchased a home in January 2014. My property taxes would be due in December 2014.  I was expecting two tax bills, one for supplemental and the other being the normal tax bill.  I received the supplemental tax bill.  I never received the normal tax bill.  I physically went to the taxing agency thinking there must be an address problem because my home was purchased earlier in the year.  I was wrong.  I never received the tax bill because the PO had returned it to the taxing agency.    Why?  I do not know.  Both the supplemental bill and the normal bill had been mailed the same day to the same address.  It turns out, the county keeps very good records on every piece of mail.  They actually gave me a document showing that the PO had returned it.  This mistake nearly cost me a substantial amount of money in penalties.

I don't know know where this mistake occurred.  It could have been in the automated sorting system or it could have been human error.  In either case, it's unacceptable.  I've tried to bring it to their attention to no avail.  Initially, I tried to call (does anyone ever answer the phone there?) as well as online (which was mostly offline).  Then I went to the PO to try and alert them that there might be a problem somewhere in the system.  Just try to get someone to listen, even with documentation.  I've always been a huge fan of the PO and have tried to support them in may ways because I want them to stay around.  But this situation certainly took them down two notches.</text>< pics>

<Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
The pumpkin bread was very good, and will try the peanut brittle next trip. The gift shop has something for everyone, and the quiet serenity of the courtyard and the chapel are very soothing, even to non-Catholics. The nuns in this order are cloistered, so you're not supposed to see them. However, we saw two nuns in the gift shop, though they might have been visitors from another location. If you're feeling troubled, and need a few moments of peace and comfort in the middle of the city, I highly recommend you  visit this little monastery.</Review>

<Date>1587515270119</Date>< text>
live in San Diego and take my bikes here...that's how incredible their service is. While I love bikes and have ridden for 12 years I know I'm not a top notch mechanic (as much as I'd like to think I am), but Lynsey and the team at Street Dreams happily took the time to walk me through my bikes status in great depth, what it could use, and what it definitely needed while being incredibly understanding and supportive the whole time. I've gotten ripped off at some shops, poor service at others, but the experience I had here was...for lack of a better word...a dream! I felt super comfortable and understood with both bikes I brought in (Triumph Scrambler and Yamaha FZ09) and the work they did on both bikes was above and beyond. Most of all I never felt in the dark, never was belittled, I knew exactly what they were doing, why, and how much it would cost throughout the whole process. This will always be the place I take any bike I own, their service makes the trek worth it!< /text>
